        </script>

          <h1>Diets to your door: Do the latest home-delivery meal packages cut the mustard?</h1> 
          <p class="author-section byline-plain">By <a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Louise+Atkinson" class="author" rel="nofollow">Louise Atkinson</a> <br> <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated"> <span class="article-timestamp-label">Updated:</span> 08:02 BST, 23 August 2010 </span> <br></p>
          <div id="articleIconLinksContainer"> 
           <ul> 
            <li class="share-facebook"></li> 
            <li class="share-twitter"></li> 
            <li class="share-pinterest"></li>

            <li class="share-email"> <a rel="nofollow" href="mailto:?subject=Read this: Diets to your door: Do the latest home-delivery meal packages cut the mustard?&amp;body=Diets%20to%20your%20door%3A%20Do%20the%20latest%20home-delivery%20meal%20packages%20cut%20the%20mustard%3F%0A%0AWe%20asked%20Dr%20Denise%20Thomas%20to%20analyse%20eight%20different%20home-delivery%20diet%20packages%2C%20and%20rate%20them%20in%20terms%20of%20their%20overall%20healthiness%20and%20their%20ability%20to%20help%20you%20lose%20weight.%0A%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fwww.dailymail.co.uk%2Ffemail%2Farticle-1305288%2FDiets-door-Do-latest-home-delivery-meal-packages-cut-mustard.html%3Fito%3Demail_share_article-top%0A%0A%0AMost%20Read%20Articles%3A%0A%0ACamilla%20%27seduced%20Charles%20to%20get%20revenge%20on%20her%20future%20husband%20Andrew%20Parker-Bowles%20who%20was%20sleeping%20with%20Anne%27%2C%20claims%20royal%20expert%20who%20says%20that%27s%20%27just%20how%20the%20upper%20class%20bonk%27%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fwww.dailymail.co.uk%2Ffemail%2Farticle-4942390%2FCamilla-got-Charles-make-husband-jealous.html%3Fito%3Demail_share_article-top_most-read-articles%0A%0A%27This%20is%20making%20my%20skin%20crawl%27%3A%20Liar%20viewers%20left%20horrified%20as%20unexpected%20twist%20sees%20pregnant%20police%20officer%20embroiled%20in%20Andrew%27s%20violent%20rampage%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fwww.dailymail.co.uk%2Ffemail%2Farticle-4941884%2FITV-Liar-sees-Andrew-attack-pregnant-woman-Laura.html%3Fito%3Demail_share_article-top_most-read-articles%0A%0AHow%20YOU%20can%20make%20%C2%A31%2C000%20before%20Christmas%3A%20Blogger%20reveals%20how%20to%20earn%20%C2%A3100%20a%20week%20from%20home%20through%20VERY%20simple%20%27side%20hustles%27%20-%20including%20audio%20typing%20and%20watching%20videos%0Ahttp%3A%2F%2Fwww.dailymail.co.uk%2Ffemail%2Farticle-4926340%2FHow-make-1-000-Christmas.html%3Fito%3Demail_share_article-top_most-read-articles%0A%0A"> <span class="wai">e-mail</span> </a> </li>

          <br>
          <p></p>
          <div class="floatRHS"> 
           <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADCC3A3000005DC-8_306x580.jpg" height="580" width="306" alt="Miracle cure: A host of new companies promise to shoulder the burden of working out what you need to eat. But can they help you lose weight in a way that's healthy?" class="blkBorder"> 
           <noscript> 
            <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADCC3A3000005DC-8_306x580.jpg" height="580" width="306" alt="Miracle cure: A host of new companies promise to shoulder the burden of working out what you need to eat. But can they help you lose weight in a way that's healthy?" class="blkBorder"> 
           </noscript> 
           <p class="imageCaption">Miracle cure: A host of new companies promise to shoulder the burden of working out what you need to eat. But can they help you lose weight healthily?<br></p>
          </div> 
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">How often have you looked enviously at the figures of the rich, famous and gorgeous, knowing the reason they're so slim and healthy is because they can afford a dedicated chef preparing nourishing, calorie-counted meals each day?&nbsp;</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Well, the good news is that the rest of us can now enjoy something similar, thanks to the ever-increasing array of home delivered diet food available. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">A host of new companies promise to shoulder the burden of working out what you need to eat, while removing the effort involved. But can they help you lose weight in a way that's healthy? </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">'These home-delivered diets do suit busy people who struggle to find the time to prepare healthy meals,' says Dr Denise Thomas, head of nutrition and dietetics at Portsmouth hospital. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">'They might stop you falling into the high-calorie trap of relying on takeaways or eating out, and they can help re-educate dieters to accept smaller portions.' </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">There are eight main home delivery diet packages on the market that deliver nationwide. Sign up, and boxes containing your diet food for a week, a few days, or just one day (depending on the plan) will arrive on your doorstep. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Some work to a standard daily calorie allowance; others calculate your personal calorie needs to plan a menu that contains 100 to 200 calories per day less, to ensure steady weight loss. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">These diet deliveries aren't a miracle cure for flab: 'Some people find losing weight easier when you limit the choice of foods like this, but successful weight management is all about lifestyle change,' warns Dr Thomas. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">However, as a way to kick-start a new regime, they can be useful.&nbsp;</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">We asked Dr Thomas to analyse the eight different home-delivery diet packages, and rate them in terms of their overall healthiness and their ability to help you lose weight. <br></font></p>
          <div class="floatRHS"> 
           <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBA2BA000005DC-831_306x195.jpg" height="195" width="306" alt="Rosemary Conley Diet" class="blkBorder"> 
           <noscript> 
            <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBA2BA000005DC-831_306x195.jpg" height="195" width="306" alt="Rosemary Conley Diet" class="blkBorder"> 
           </noscript> 
           <p class="imageCaption">Balanced: Rosemary Conley's chicken hot pot<br></p>
          </div> 
          <p style="font-weight: bold; color: rgb(212, 38, 153);"><font style="font-size: 1.6em;">SOLO SLIM</font></p>
          <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">Cost: 6.71 per day. Visit www.rosemaryconley.com or call 0870 0507 727 </font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get:</span> One week's diet&nbsp; -&nbsp; a cereal bar and a sachet of hot chocolate per day, a low-fat soup and a ready meal such as lowfat chicken hot pot or low-fat chilli and rice in a microwaveable pouch. There is also a 200g block of low-fat cheese to last the week. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add:</span> A bowl of high-fibre breakfast cereal each day, three portions of fruit or vegetables/salad, 3/4 pint of milk, 1-2 slices of wholegrain bread, and low-fat yoghurt to make up a calorie total of 1,200 per day. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Support: </span>No initial consultation or helpline, but it's easy to tap into Conley's media empire with TV shows, websites and interactive forums available. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise: </span>Not mentioned with this plan, but very much part of the Rosemary Conley message. Lots of advice on the website. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility:</span> Vegetarian option available, and there's a choice of five soups, ten meals and three different cereal bars in your box. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Taste verdict:</span> Soups are tasty and evening meals are palatable and filling when bulked up with two portions of veg. The cereal bar is too sweet and, at 65 calories a cup, the hot chocolate is twice as calorific as many diet versions. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view: </span>This balanced, low-fat diet is the sort of plan most health professionals would recommend for weight loss. It's a low cost, stripped-down service backed by years of experience. Adding your own elements gives freedom, but also a wide margin for cheating&nbsp; -&nbsp; it would be tempting to add extra cheese. The calorie count for the evening meals varies, so the meal you select could make an impact on daily total. <br><br style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">VERDICT: 7/10</span><br></font></p>
          <div class="floatRHS"> 
           <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADC55D8000005DC-58_306x236.jpg" height="236" width="306" alt="Not recommended without medical supervision: You get three milkshakes per day" class="blkBorder"> 
           <noscript> 
            <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADC55D8000005DC-58_306x236.jpg" height="236" width="306" alt="Not recommended without medical supervision: You get three milkshakes per day" class="blkBorder"> 
           </noscript> 
           <p class="imageCaption">Not recommended without medical supervision: You get three milkshakes per day but the low calories could make you feel light-headed<br></p>
          </div> 
          <p style="font-weight: bold; color: rgb(212, 38, 153);"><font style="font-size: 1.6em;">WEIGHT TO GO</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;">Cost: 8.71 per day. Visit www.weightogo.com or 0845 468 1280 </font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span><br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get</span>: Three milkshakes per day (one for breakfast and two snacks), a pouch of soup, a ready meal (such as chilli with rustic Camargue red rice, or chickpea and sweet potato tagine) for supper and two energy bars per week. It's delivered weekly (or as a four-week 'value' box). <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add:</span> </font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">One portion </font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">of fruit and vegetables, to make a total of 850 calories per day. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Support: </span>No initial consultation unless requested, but you can call or email a 'health educator, leave a message and should receive a reply within 24 hours. You have access to a dedicated blog and receive a regular newsletter, but advisers do not track individual weight loss. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise:</span> You are urged to take a brisk, 30-minute walk each day </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility:</span> There's a 'weekend off' box on offer, so you can have a break from the diet two days a week. After your first order you can pick the soups and meals you prefer (from five soups and eight main meals), and order individual elements (shake powders and snack bars) separately. Vegetarian or wheat-free diet options available.&nbsp;</font></p>
          <p><span style="font-weight: bold;">T</span><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">aste verdict: </span>Acceptable soups, but main meals taste like Army rations, and the thick, very sweet milk shakes are barely palatable. energy bars taste artificial and are too sweet. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view: </span>Low-calorie diets like this are not recommended without medical supervision. The high-protein shakes might help you feel full, but on 850 calories per day you're likely be light-headed and tired. Very little support considering how hard it is to stick to. You may lose weight rapidly, but this would be difficult to maintain.&nbsp;</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">VERDICT: 3/10</span></font></p>
          <div class="feMailHeaderWide"> 
           <div class="floatRHS"> 
            <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBCCDF000005DC-76_306x206.jpg" height="206" width="306" alt="Pure Package dinner" class="blkBorder"> 
            <noscript> 
             <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBCCDF000005DC-76_306x206.jpg" height="206" width="306" alt="Pure Package dinner" class="blkBorder"> 
            </noscript> 
            <p class="imageCaption">Delicious: All food is unprocessed and unrefined <font style="font-size: 1.2em;"></font></p>
           </div> 
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.6em;">THE PURE PACKAGE</font></p>
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">Cost: 36.95 per day, from 08456 123888 and www.purepackage.com&nbsp; -&nbsp; not easily available outside Greater London </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get:</span> A cool bag delivered every morning containing breakfast ( for example, granola with goat's milk yoghurt and berries), two fresh organic meals (fish with vegetables, goats cheese and butternut squash salad), and individually packaged snacks (oat cakes with tapenade, a piece of fruit a small sachet of nuts or seeds). All food is unprocessed and unrefined. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add:</span> Nothing. Your cool bag contains 1,200 to 1,500 calories per day, with a different menu each day personalised to your tastes and lifestyle. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Support:</span> Kicks off with an in- depth telephone consultation, so the diet can be individually tailored. Then the consultant calls regularly to check progress and offer help&nbsp; -&nbsp; if you are going to a restaurant, tell the team, they'll contact the restaurant, look at the menu, and advise accordingly. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise</span>: not emphasised </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility</span>: The weight-loss programme is one of many options, including healthy eating, anti-ageing, brain balance and detox plans. Portion sizes can be altered to suit individual appetites and dinners for partner or friend are available at 9.50 a time. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">Costs can be reduced by opting for a no-breakfast, no-dinner or no-lunch programme. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Taste verdict</span>: Delicious and beautifully presented. each meal is laid-out in a sealed tray with pots of dips and dressings, and bags of nuts and seeds. The closest thing to having your own diet chef. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view:</span> This diet is very balanced and nutritious. Frequent small meals balance blood sugar levels to help you lose weight, and reduce cravings and mood swings. At around 1,500 calories per day you should lose 1lb of weight a week, which is good. The support is solid, too, but the plan is definitely unhealthy for the wallet. <br></font></p>
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">VERDICT: 9/10<br></font></p>
          </div> 
          <div class="floatRHS"> 
           <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBD54A000005DC-328_306x230.jpg" height="230" width="306" alt="Brocolli Soup" class="blkBorder"> 
           <noscript> 
            <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBD54A000005DC-328_306x230.jpg" height="230" width="306" alt="Brocolli Soup" class="blkBorder"> 
           </noscript> 
           <p class="imageCaption">Generous portions: You could end up eating more calories and slow your weight loss<font style="font-size: 1.2em;"></font></p>
          </div> 
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.6em; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(212, 38, 153);">NKD</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;">Cost: 9.28 per day. Visit www.nkddiet.co.uk or call 020 7193 6410</font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">&nbsp;</span><br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get: </span>A week's supply containing breakfast (sachet of porridge oats or granola), lunch (soup or pasta salad), and an evening meal (such as beef casserole, or chana massala) plus a snack (two plain rice cakes or low-cal biscuits). </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add: </span>One portion of fruit and one of vegetables and either milk or low-fat yoghurt with your breakfast, to make a daily total of 1,000 calories. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Support:</span> You can buy online, or phone to cherry-pick food choices and personalise your menu. Optional phone consultation includes questions on current weight, weight-loss goals, dietary requirements and activity levels. The food box comes with a comprehensive weight-loss handbook with useful advice. Unlimited use of telephone support line and a weekly call from your dedicated 'weight loss professional'. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise:</span> Lots of encouragement to exercise, with exercise log pages in handbook. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility:</span> Choose the meals you prefer and higher protein or vegetarian menus can be devised. Option to buy extra evening meals, so you and your partner can eat together. Free replacement if you don't like a meal. Money back if you don't like the plan. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Taste verdict:</span> Breakfast portions are tiny, but the soups are delicious and meals hearty, tasty and very varied&nbsp; -&nbsp; in fact, not diet food at all&nbsp; -&nbsp; many are re-labelled supermarket ready-meals. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view:</span> Although you could easily buy this food yourself at the supermarket , the programme offers exceptional support. The meals seem generous in comparison to other plans, so be careful or you could end up eating more calories on some days and slow your weight loss.&nbsp;</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">VERDICT: 8/10</span></font><br><br><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span></font></p>
          <div class="feMailHeaderWide">
           <div class="floatRHS"> 
            <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBA37E000005DC-199_306x355.jpg" height="355" width="306" alt="Soulmate" class="blkBorder"> 
            <noscript> 
             <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBA37E000005DC-199_306x355.jpg" height="355" width="306" alt="Soulmate" class="blkBorder"> 
            </noscript> 
            <p class="imageCaption">Soul food: Luxurious and impossible to feel deprived</p>
           </div> 
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.6em;">SOULMATE FOOD</font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;">Cost: 25 per day (min six-day order) www.soulmatefood.com or 0870 803 3833 </font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span><br></font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get:</span> An insulated box with three days' worth of fresh, organic, low-fat, wholegrain food, with three varied main courses (such as Thai chicken noodle salad or swordfish with black bean salsa) and two snacks, plus a collection of vitamin and mineral supplements. Each menu is bespoke and the calorie count individually calculated. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add:</span> Nothing. </font></p> 
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Support:</span> A telephone consultation establishes your typical diet, activity levels and any intolerances or dislikes. You have unlimited phone and email access to staff including nutritionists. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise:</span> Free phone advice from personal trainers. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility:</span> You can eliminate food groups and up to three foods you don't like. In addition to the weight loss plan, you could choose a two-week detox or anti-cellulite package. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Taste verdict:</span> Generous portions (huge plate of wholemeal noodles with 15 big fat prawns on top), lots of snacks and treats ( such as four large strawberries dipped in chocolate). Luxurious and impossible to feel deprived. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view:</span> This is an expensive way to eat healthily, but provides a great education in terms of portion size, new combinations, and how to spread meals and snacks throughout the day. Weight loss would be steady and more likely to last.</font></p>
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">VERDICT: 9/10<br> </font></p> 
          </div> 
          <div class="floatRHS"> 
           <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0AE2028A000005DC-632_306x285.jpg" height="285" width="306" alt="Yoghurt with fresh berries in small bowl" class="blkBorder"> 
           <noscript> 
            <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0AE2028A000005DC-632_306x285.jpg" height="285" width="306" alt="Yoghurt with fresh berries in small bowl" class="blkBorder"> 
           </noscript> 
           <p class="imageCaption">Atkins by post: Add your own yoghurt and berries to the sachet of breakfast cereal<br></p>
          </div> 
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.6em; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(212, 38, 153);">GO LOWER</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;">Cost: 10 per day (7.23 per day if you pay for 8 weeks) www.golower.co.uk or call 0800 862 0099</font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">&nbsp;</span><br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get:</span> Weekly or monthly delivery. Each day you get a sachet of breakfast cereal, soup or a portion of sliced salami with dressing for lunch, and a low-carb ready meal such as beef in thyme gravy or chicken and leeks in a cream sauce for the evening, plus two snacks a day. This is Atkins by post: high-protein, high-fat, but very low-carb. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add:</span> Milk or Greek yoghurt and berries to breakfast, salad at lunch and vegetables with supper. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Support: </span>You will be allocated a personal consultant, who performs the initial consultation and is then available for support (by </font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">phone, email, text). A trained nutritionist is available seven days a week through an appointments system and you can access a members' forum. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise: </span>The plan recommends weight training for toning up. <br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility:</span> After 14 to 28 days, you move into the steady weightloss phase and can customise the meal choice and add treats (chocolate-coated Brazil nuts, chocolate mousse). Your progress is constantly monitored and your diet adjusted accordingly. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Taste verdict: </span>The breakfast granola and cereal bars are more nutty than sweet, and the soups and main meals are rich and tasty. There's more meat than the other plans, but I found myself eating the thin, oily meatball sauce wishing I had a potato to soak it up. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view:</span> Few health professionals will endorse Atkins-style diets like this one, because they are designed to kickstart ketosis to burn fat by cutting out carbohydrates. During ketosis, the body produces chemicals called ketones, which are poisonous and affect your blood chemistry, which is why you can feel ill during the early stages of these diets. Although these low-carb diets can be effective in the short term and this plan is not expensive, I would stress caution. </font><br><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">VERDICT: 3/10</span></font><br></p>
          <div class="floatRHS"> 
           <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0AE20286000005DC-32_306x192.jpg" height="192" width="306" alt="Fried rice with vegetables and egg" class="blkBorder"> 
           <noscript> 
            <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0AE20286000005DC-32_306x192.jpg" height="192" width="306" alt="Fried rice with vegetables and egg" class="blkBorder"> 
           </noscript> 
           <p class="imageCaption">Only good for short term: Once you start eating solid food in the evenings, you may find it difficult to stop</p>
          </div> 
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.6em; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(212, 38, 153);">NOSH DETOX</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;">Cost: 50.90 per day for a minimum of six days. Visit noshdetoxdelivery.com, 0845 257 6674</font><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">&nbsp;</span><br></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get:</span> Large smoothie for breakfast, mid-morning vitamin smoothie, soup for lunch, small smoothie mid-afternoon, then a light organic, gluten and dairy free cooked supper (such as stir-fried rice and vegetables or bacon and pea risotto with watercress) to total 1,200-1,500 calories per day. Deliveries within M25 are fresh to the door each evening. Various nationwide options available. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add:</span> Fresh ginger and lemon to make into a hot drink to start the day, and herbal teas. </font><br><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">support: There's an optional initial phone consultation, but an online form asks about allergies and intolerances. You can call or email questions and a nutritionist will reply. Everyone gets a tenminute consultation with a nutritionist. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise</span>: Plan recommends light, gentle exercise such as yoga, swimming and gentle jogging, and suggests a tenminute walk each day. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility:</span> The alternatives include a sixday juice fast or healthy ( nondiet) food. Can be tailored for people with food intolerances. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Taste verdict: </span>The breakfast smoothie tasted healthy rather than fabulous, and the rest were delicious but small. The spicy pumpkin soup was tasty but only just filled a medium-sized mug. And although the evening meal was bursting with flavour, the portion was not filling. </font><br></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view: </span>A very-low calorie liquid diet followed by a balanced meal in the evening means you may feel light-headed until the evening meal. And once you start eating solid food in the evenings, you may find it difficult to stop. Generally, meal replacement diets like this do well, but long-term benefits are doubtful.&nbsp;</font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">VERDICT: 5/10</span></font><br><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span></font></p>
          <div class="feMailHeaderWide">
           <div class="floatRHS"> 
            <img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBD23E000005DC-406_306x248.jpg" height="248" width="306" alt="mushroom_risotto" class="blkBorder"> 
            <noscript> 
             <img src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2010/08/22/article-1305288-0ADBD23E000005DC-406_306x248.jpg" height="248" width="306" alt="mushroom_risotto" class="blkBorder"> 
            </noscript> 
            <p class="imageCaption">Healthy: Food is portioned but not restrictive<br></p>
           </div> 
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.6em;">DIET CHEF</font></p>
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.4em;">Cost: 7.49 per day. Visit www.dietchef.co.uk or 0845 094 9796 </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you get:</span> Granola or flavoured porridge, soup or milkshake for lunch and a readymeal such as beef bolognese ( no pasta), pork meatballs, or chicken casserole for dinner, plus a snack (such as a two-pack of oat biscuits). Weekly, fortnightly or monthly. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">What you add:</span> A portion of fruit and veg plus semi-skimmed milk or a small pot of yoghurt per day to make a total of 1,200 calories (or 1,500 calories if very active). </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Support:</span> An online quiz takes your height, weight and activity levels and estimates how many calories you need for steady weight loss. Support comes in the form of monthly email tips and hints, and, if you have problems, you can get into a rather stilted online live chat with a Diet Chef representative. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Exercise:</span> Not essential but strongly recommended. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Flexibility: </span>Choose what you want for breakfast, lunch and supper. More options for active dieters and vegetarians. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Taste verdict:</span> A huge choice of delicious soups and a variety of long-life microwaveable meals for supper. </font></p>
           <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Expert view: </span>A good healthy plan that would help you lose weight. The food is portioned but not restrictive and the energy levels per meal are good. Although the level of support is not as comprehensive as some other plans, its Facebook page is a good way of keeping customers on track. <br></font></p>
           <p style="font-weight: bold;"><font style="font-size: 1.2em;">VERDICT: 7/10</font></p>
          </div> 
          <p><br><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span></font></p>
          <p><br><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"></span></font></p>
          <p><font style="font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><br></span></font></p>

        <script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 0;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n,
                target_type: 'mix'
            });
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=femail&pageSize=10',
            total: 20.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
